\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}Base class for all kernels.

.. versionadded:: 0.18

Examples
--------
>>> from sklearn.gaussian_process.kernels import Kernel, RBF
>>> import numpy as np
>>> class CustomKernel(Kernel):
...     def __init__(self, length_scale=1.0):
...         self.length_scale = length_scale
...     def __call__(self, X, Y=None):
...         if Y is None:
...             Y = X
...         return np.inner(X, X if Y is None else Y) ** 2
...     def diag(self, X):
...         return np.ones(X.shape[0])
...     def is_stationary(self):
...         return True
>>> kernel = CustomKernel(length_scale=2.0)
>>> X = np.array([[1, 2], [3, 4]])
>>> print(kernel(X))
[[ 25 121]
 [121 625]]
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Returns the log-transformed bounds on the theta.

Returns
-------
bounds : ndarray of shape (n_dims, 2)
    The log-transformed bounds on the kernel's hyperparameters theta
\end{DoxyVerb}

\index{diag@{diag}!sklearn.gaussian\_process.kernels.Kernel@{sklearn.gaussian\_process.kernels.Kernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{diag()}{diag()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1Kernel_a0d6d613c6a03a8bf2d1d0532a9881a73} 
sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Kernel.\+diag (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{X}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Returns the diagonal of the kernel k(X, X).

The result of this method is identical to np.diag(self(X)); however,
it can be evaluated more efficiently since only the diagonal is
evaluated.

Parameters
----------
X : array-like of shape (n_samples,)
    Left argument of the returned kernel k(X, Y)

Returns
-------
K_diag : ndarray of shape (n_samples_X,)
    Diagonal of kernel k(X, X)
\end{DoxyVerb}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_params()}{set\_params()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1Kernel_a3f0d35e42bd2d2f215f410b7d3c737e9} 
sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Kernel.\+set\+\_\+params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{params}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set the parameters of this kernel.

The method works on simple kernels as well as on nested kernels.
The latter have parameters of the form ``<component>__<parameter>``
so that it's possible to update each component of a nested object.

Returns
-------
self
\end{DoxyVerb}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{theta()}{theta()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1Kernel_a6ef5589e27b501f8605422e0419b4e7f} 
sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Kernel.\+theta (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Returns the (flattened, log-transformed) non-fixed hyperparameters.

Note that theta are typically the log-transformed values of the
kernel's hyperparameters as this representation of the search space
is more amenable for hyperparameter search, as hyperparameters like
length-scales naturally live on a log-scale.

Returns
-------
theta : ndarray of shape (n_dims,)
    The non-fixed, log-transformed hyperparameters of the kernel
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1CompoundKernel_ad3e77b41362edf02baf71bd3d40b3c17}{sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Compound\+Kernel}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1CompoundKernel_ab724cd275b42045c2bb900ea336819dd}{sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Compound\+Kernel}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1Exponentiation_a4c0e45d7388ad4b8a7f64ef557c9b37a}{sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Exponentiation}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1Exponentiation_a3dc7cd8c401a6da2bfd4a8e919138f1e}{sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Exponentiation}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1KernelOperator_a8549936be45397655cb6750856073cee}{sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Kernel\+Operator}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classsklearn_1_1gaussian__process_1_1kernels_1_1KernelOperator_ab6bace0bc2691577f891c0dd2414d3db}{sklearn.\+gaussian\+\_\+process.\+kernels.\+Kernel\+Operator}}.
